#第三国际邀请
FRA_intern_invite_soc = {
	intern_invite = {
		icon = hand_out
		visible = {
			tag = FRA
			has_global_flag = FRA_created_phalanstere
		}
		available = {
			tag = FRA
			has_global_flag = FRA_created_phalanstere
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_government = totalist
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
				NOT = { has_war_with = FRA }
				exists = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = INT_has_the_effects }
				NOT = { tag = USA }
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				INT_get_the_effects = yes
				country_event = comfrance.127
				force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#经济建设
FRA_eco_develop = {
	FRA_jaco_eco_hd1 = {
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			FROM = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 3
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
		icon = factories
	    cost = 40
		days_remove = 60
		fire_only_once = yes
		state_target = yes
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 4 }
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

#国家道路网络
FRA_national_road_network_system_build = {
	FRA_build_the_system_show = {
		allowed = { always = yes }
		visible = {
			tag = FRA
			FRA = { has_completed_focus = FRA_national_road_network }
		}
		cost = 0
		days_re_enable = 0
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = build_the_system_show }
				clr_country_flag = build_the_system_show
			}
			else = { set_country_flag = build_the_system_show }
		}
	}

	FRA_build_the_system = {
		allowed = { always = yes }
		visible = { has_country_flag = build_the_system_show }
		icon = road
		available = {
			tag = FRA
			FRA = { has_completed_focus = FRA_national_road_network }
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 5 }
		cost = 15
		days_remove = 60
		fire_only_once = yes
		state_target = yes
		modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 2 }
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = { 
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = FRA_national_road_network_system } 
			}
		}
	}
}

			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_stability < 0 } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { possp = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_stability < 0.1 } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { possp = 15 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_stability < 0.2 } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { possp = 10 }
			}
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = possp
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
			random = {
				chance = var:FRA.possp

				}
			}		
		}

				has_war_with = GEA
			}
		}
		available = {

					AND = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = GEA }
					}
					exists = no
				}
			}	
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 600
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_mission_inc_revo_tips
			if = {
				limit = {
					INC = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = GEA }
					}			
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ieuc = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { iasc = 20 }
				set_temp_variable = { imec = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { iamc = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { iafc = 0 }
				infulence_change_total = yes
				GEA = { add_stability = -0.1 }
				DEI = { add_stability = -0.1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { INC = { exists = no } }
				set_temp_variable = { ieuc = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { iasc = -15 }
				set_temp_variable = { imec = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { iamc = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { iafc = 0 }
				infulence_change_total = yes
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { ieuc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { iasc = -15 }
			set_temp_variable = { imec = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { iamc = 0 }

			custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_me_ottoman_kurdistan_revo_tips
		}
		remove_effect = {
			set_global_flag = FRA_kurdistan_revolution

				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 350
						state = 352
						state = 819
					}
					compliance < 5
					resistance > 60
				}
				transfer_state_to = KUR
			}
			KUR = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { FRA.kur_socialism > 40 } }
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						last_election = "1888.6.15"
						election_frequency = 48
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
						last_election = "1888.6.15"
						election_frequency = 48
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}	
				add_ideas = KUR_brother_behind_brother
				declare_war_on = {
					target = OTT
					type = annex_everything
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = internvene.118 days = 360 }

					set_temp_variable = { t = FRA.kur_nationalism }
					set_temp_variable = { t1 = t }
					multiply_temp_variable = { t1 = 0.6 }
					set_temp_variable = { t2 = t }
					multiply_temp_variable = { t2 = 0.2 }
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = FRA.kur_socialism
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 0
						social_liberal = 0
						market_liberal = 0
						social_conservative = t2
						authoritarian_democrat = t2
						paternal_autocrat = t1
						national_populist = 0
					}					
					division_template = {
						name = "Dabeskirina Mizgefte"
						division_names_group = OTT_INF_01
						is_locked = no
						regiments = {
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
	
					every_owned_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Dabeskirina Mizgefte\" division_template = \"Dabeskirina Mizgefte\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"

					add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.075 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_stability < 0.2 } }
					add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.05 }
				}
				else = { add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.025 } }
			}
		}
	}

		allowed = { always = no }
		visible = { has_country_flag = synd_trav_goals }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FRA_politics_synd_trav_union_cost_tips
				check_variable = { FRA_synd_trav_union > 30 }
			}
		}
		cost = 10
		days_re_enable = 15
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { uc = -5 }
			FRA_synd_trav_union_change = yes

			set_temp_variable = { FRA_politics_points_change = 30 }
			FRA_politics_points_change = yes

			set_temp_variable = { times = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { numbers = 2.5 }
			random_faction_satisfation_plus = yes
		}
	}

	FRA_politics_synd_trav_union_gain = {
		icon = generic_flags
		allowed = { always = no }
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = synd_trav_goals
		}
		custom_cost_text = FRA_politics_points_ten
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			check_variable = { FRA_politics_points > 9 }
		}
		days_re_enable = 30
		fixed_random_seed = no
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { FRA_politics_points_change = -10 }
			FRA_politics_points_change = yes
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					set_temp_variable = { uc = 15 }
					FRA_synd_trav_union_change = yes
				}
				2 = {
					set_temp_variable = { uc = 10 }
					FRA_synd_trav_union_change = yes
				}
				1 = {
					set_temp_variable = { uc = 5 }
					FRA_synd_trav_union_change = yes
				}
			}	

			set_temp_variable = { stabt = frasoc_synd }
			add_to_temp_variable = { stabt = frasoc_anar }
			add_to_temp_variable = { stabt = frasoc_jaco }
			add_to_temp_variable = { stabt = frasoc_sore }
			divide_temp_variable = { stabt = 4 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabt = 0.001 }

			add_stability = var:FRA.stabt
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = synd_trav_union_member_radi
					check_variable = { seat_synd_radi > 80 }
					check_variable = { frasoc_synd > 40 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { t = seat_synd_radi }
				divide_temp_variable = { t = 80 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { t = frasoc_synd }
				multiply_temp_variable = { t = 0.1 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { t = 5 }
				set_temp_variable = { FRA_politics_points_change = t }
				FRA_politics_points_change = yes
			}
		}
	}

	FRA_politics_synd_trav_compromise = {
		icon = peace_dove
		allowed = { always = no }
		visible = { has_country_flag = synd_trav_goals }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FRA_politics_synd_trav_compromise_tips
				check_variable = {
					FRA_synd_trav_union > 80
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 60
		days_remove = 150
		days_re_enable = 170
		modifier = { 
			political_power_gain = 0.5
			stability_weekly = 0.005
			war_support_weekly = 0.005
			army_core_attack_factor = 0.2			
			army_core_defence_factor = 0.2
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { uc = -5 }
			FRA_synd_trav_union_change = yes

			set_temp_variable = { stcc = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { seat_synd_radi > 10 } }
				set_temp_variable = { src = -5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { stcc = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { seat_indenpent > 10 } }
				set_temp_variable = { sindc = -5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { stcc = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { seat_anar_parl > 10 } }
				set_temp_variable = { apc = -5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { stcc = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { seat_anar_anar > 10 } }
				set_temp_variable = { aac = -5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { stcc = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = synd_trav_union_member_neos
					check_variable = { seat_jaco_neos > 10 } 
				}
				set_temp_variable = { jnc = -5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { stcc = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = synd_trav_union_member_leni
					check_variable = { seat_jaco_leni > 10 } 
				}
				set_temp_variable = { jlc = -5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { stcc = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = synd_trav_union_member_oldl
					check_variable = { seat_sore_oldl > 10 } 
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soc = -5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { stcc = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = synd_trav_union_member_yout
					check_variable = { seat_sore_yout > 10 } 
				}
				set_temp_variable = { syc = -5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { stcc = 1 }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { stcc = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { stc = stcc }
			FRA_seat_change = yes
		}
	}

	FRA_synd_radi_anti_change = {
		icon = oppression
		allowed = {
			always = no
			tag = FRA
		}
		available = { has_country_flag = synd_radi_no_change }
		is_good = yes
		fixed_random_seed = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { t = synd_radi_goals_anti }
			multiply_temp_variable = { t = -0.02 }
			set_temp_variable = { wc = t }
			set_temp_variable = { pc = t }
			set_temp_variable = { mc = t }
			set_temp_variable = { sc = t }
			set_temp_variable = { fc = t }
			set_temp_variable = { bc = t }
			FRA_social_politic_situation_change = yes			

			set_variable = { anticmax = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { anticmax = anticc }
			set_temp_variable_to_random = { var = antic max = var:FRA.antimax min = 1 }

			set_variable = { intensecmax = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { intensecmax = intensecc }
			set_temp_variable_to_random = { var = intensec max = var:FRA.intensecmax min = -2 }

			set_variable = { boredomcmax = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { boredomcmax = boredomcc }
			set_temp_variable_to_random = { var = boredomc max = var:FRA.boredomcmax min = -2 }
			
			FRA_synd_radi_goals_change = yes

			random_list = {
				var:FRA.frasoc_total = { }
				100 = {
					modifier = {
						set_temp_variable = { t = var:FRA.frasoc_totoal }
						multiply_temp_variable = { t = -1 }
						add = t
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = frapoc121one
					add_to_variable = { anticc = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { intensecc = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { boredomcc = 1 }
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = { activate_mission = FRA_synd_radi_anti_change }	
		}	
	}

			set_temp_variable = { t = cule }
			multiply_temp_variable = { t = -2.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { antic = t }
			set_temp_variable = { q = cule }
			multiply_temp_variable = { q = 1.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { intensec = q } 
			set_temp_variable = { boredomc = 0 } 
			FRA_synd_radi_goals_change = yes
			set_variable = { temp_cule = cule }
			set_variable = { cule = 0 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			multiply_variable = { temp_cule = 0.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { wc = temp_cule }
			set_temp_variable = { pc = temp_cule }
			set_temp_variable = { mc = temp_cule }
			set_temp_variable = { sc = temp_cule }
			set_temp_variable = { fc = temp_cule }
			set_temp_variable = { bc = temp_cule }
			FRA_social_politic_situation_change = yes
			set_variable = { temp_cule = 0 }
		}
	}

	FRA_politics_anar_parl_change = {
		icon = ger_mefo_bills
		allowed = {
			always = no
			tag = FRA
		}
		available = { always = no }
		is_good = yes
		fixed_random_seed = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { ppcc = var:FRA.party_popularity_100@totalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ppcc = var:FRA.party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ppcc = 0.1 }
			set_temp_variable = { ppc = ppcc }
		
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { parl_system_power > 50 } }
				set_temp_variable = { picc = parl_system_power }
				add_to_temp_variable = { picc = -50 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { picc = 0.1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { parl_system_power < 50 } }
				set_temp_variable = { picc = parl_system_power }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { picc = 50 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { picc = 0.1 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { t = parl_system_willing }
			multiply_temp_variable = { t = -0.1 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { picc = t }
			set_temp_variable = { pic = picc }
			
			set_temp_variable = { pwcc = frasoc_jaco }
			add_to_temp_variable = { pwcc = frasoc_sore }
			multiply_temp_variable = { pwcc = 0.25 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { pwcc = -50 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { pwcc = 0.1 }
			set_temp_variable = { pwc = pwcc }
			FRA_anar_parl_goals_change = yes

			hidden_effect = { activate_mission = FRA_politics_anar_parl_change }	
		}	
	}

	FRA_politic_jaco_neos_goals_change = {
		icon = ger_mefo_bills
		allowed = {
			always = no
			tag = FRA
		}
		available = { always = no }
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { jttc = jaco_techbure_train }
			add_to_temp_variable = { jttc = -40 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { jttc = 0.05 }
			
			set_temp_variable = { jtapc = jaco_techbure_appiont }
			add_to_temp_variable = { jtapc = -40 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { jtapc = 0.05 }

			set_temp_variable = { jtacc = jaco_techbure_account }
			add_to_temp_variable = { jtacc = -40 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { jtacc = 0.05 }

			set_temp_variable = { jaco_techbure_progressc = jttc }
			add_to_temp_variable = { jaco_techbure_progressc = jtapc }
			add_to_temp_variable = { jaco_techbure_progressc = jtacc }
			FRA_jaco_neos_goals_change = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tmc = jaco_techbure_train }
			add_to_temp_variable = { tmc = -50 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { tmc = -0.02 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { tmc = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { tec = jaco_techbure_train }
			add_to_temp_variable = { tec = -50 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { tec = 0.04 }

			set_temp_variable = { apmc = jaco_techbure_appiont }
			add_to_temp_variable = { apmc = -50 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { apmc = -0.04 }
			set_temp_variable = { appc = jaco_techbure_appiont }
			add_to_temp_variable = { appc = -50 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { appc = -0.04 }

			set_temp_variable = { acec = jaco_techbure_account }
			add_to_temp_variable = { acec = -50 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { acec = 0.04 }
			set_temp_variable = { acpc = jaco_techbure_account }
			add_to_temp_variable = { acpc = -50 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { acpc = -0.04 }

			set_temp_variable = { c = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { m = tmc }
			add_to_temp_variable = { m = apmc }
			set_temp_variable = { e = tec }
			add_to_temp_variable = { e = acec }
			set_temp_variable = { p = appc }
			add_to_temp_variable = { p = acpc }
			set_temp_variable = { s = 0 }
			FRA_govern_single_change = yes

			hidden_effect = { activate_mission = FRA_politic_jaco_neos_goals_change }	
		}	
	}

	FRA_politics_sore_oldl_interventionism = {
		icon = global_trade
		allowed = { always = no }
		visible = { has_country_flag = sore_oldl_goals }

		days_remove = 60

			set_country_flag = has_choosen_sore_propoganda

				limit = { 
					OR = {
						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism = 20 } 
						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism < 20 } 
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soit1 = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { soit2 = 1 } 	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism > 20 }
					OR = {
						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism = 40 } 
						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism < 40 }
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soit1 = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { soit2 = 2 } 	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism > 40 }
					OR = {
						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism = 60 } 
						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism < 60 }
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soit1 = 3 }
				set_temp_variable = { soit2 = 3 } 	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism > 60 }
					OR = {

						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism < 80 }
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soit1 = 4 }

						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism = 100 } 
						check_variable = { sore_oldl_interventionism < 100 }
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soit1 = 5 }
				set_temp_variable = { soit2 = 5 } 	
			}
			
			set_variable = { sont1 = 0 }
			set_variable = { sont2 = 0 }
			set_variable = { somt1 = 0 }
			set_variable = { somt2 = 0 }
			set_variable = { soit1 = 0 }
			set_variable = { soit2 = 0 }
			set_variable = { soit3 = 0 }
			set_variable = { soit4 = 0 }
			set_variable = { sost1 = 0 }
			set_variable = { sost2 = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { soit3 = sore_oldl_interventionism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { soit3 = -0.003 }
			set_temp_variable = { soit4 = sore_oldl_interventionism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { soit4 = 0.002 }

				multiply_variable = { soit3 = -0.003 }
				set_variable = { soit4 = sore_oldl_interventionism }
				multiply_variable = { soit4 = 0.002 }
			}

				}

					limit = { has_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_fade }
					custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_politics_sore_oldl_flame_close
					set_temp_variable = { sonc = -5 }
					set_temp_variable = { somc = -5 }					
					set_temp_variable = { soic = -5 }
					set_temp_variable = { sosc = -5 }

					set_temp_variable = { sowewc = -2 }

	FRA_politics_sore_oldl_fire_flame = {
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
		allowed = {
			always = no
			tag = FRA
		}
		available = { has_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_closed	}
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		timeout_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { sonc = soncc }
			set_temp_variable = { somc = somcc }
			set_temp_variable = { soic = soicc }
			set_temp_variable = { sosc = soscc }
			set_temp_variable = { sowec = sowec }
			set_temp_variable = { sowewc = sowewcc }
			FRA_sore_oldl_goals_change = yes

			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_opened }
				set_variable = { magnt = sore_oldl_war_engine }
				multiply_variable = { magnt = 0.005 }
				add_to_variable = { magnt = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_fire }
				set_variable = { magnt = sore_oldl_war_engine }
				multiply_variable = { magnt = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { magnt = 1 }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_opened 
						has_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_fire
					}
				}
				set_variable = { magnt = sore_oldl_war_engine }
				multiply_variable = { magnt = 0.005 }
				add_to_variable = { magnt = 1 }

				set_variable = { nationt1 = sore_oldl_nationalism }
				multiply_variable = { nationt1 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { nationt1 = -0.2 }
				multiply_variable = { nationt1 = magnt }

				set_variable = { nationt2 = sore_oldl_nationalism }
				multiply_variable = { nationt2 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { nationt2 = 0.2 }
				multiply_variable = { nationt2 = magnt }

				set_variable = { militart1 = sore_oldl_militarism }
				multiply_variable = { militart1 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { militart1 = 0.1 }
				multiply_variable = { militart1 = magnt }

				set_variable = { militart2 = sore_oldl_militarism }
				multiply_variable = { militart2 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { militart2 = 0.1 }
				multiply_variable = { militart2 = magnt }

				set_variable = { intert1 = sore_oldl_interventionism }
				multiply_variable = { intert1 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { intert1 = 0.15 }
				multiply_variable = { intert1 = magnt }

				set_variable = { intert2 = sore_oldl_interventionism }
				multiply_variable = { intert2 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { intert2 = 0.15 }
				multiply_variable = { intert2 = magnt }

				set_variable = { socialt1 = sore_oldl_socialism }
				multiply_variable = { socialt1 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { socialt1 = 0.1 }
				multiply_variable = { socialt1 = magnt }
				
				set_variable = { socialt2 = sore_oldl_socialism }
				multiply_variable = { socialt2 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { socialt2 = 0.15 }
				multiply_variable = { socialt2 = magnt }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_fade }
				set_variable = { nationt1 = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { nationt1 = sore_oldl_nationalism }
				multiply_variable = { nationt1 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { nationt1 = 0.2 }

				set_variable = { nationt2 = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { nationt2 = sore_oldl_nationalism }
				multiply_variable = { nationt2 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { nationt2 = -0.2 }

				set_variable = { militart1 = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { militart1 = sore_oldl_militarism }
				multiply_variable = { militart1 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { militart1 = -0.2 }

				set_variable = { militart2 = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { militart2 = sore_oldl_militarism }
				multiply_variable = { militart2 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { militart2 = 0.2 }

				set_variable = { intert1 = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { intert1 = sore_oldl_interventionism }
				multiply_variable = { intert1 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { intert1 = -0.2 }

				set_variable = { intert2 = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { intert2 = sore_oldl_interventionism }
				multiply_variable = { intert2 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { intert2 = -0.2 }

				set_variable = { socialt1 = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { socialt1 = sore_oldl_socialism }
				multiply_variable = { socialt1 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { socialt1 = -0.2 }
				
				set_variable = { socialt2 = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { socialt2 = sore_oldl_socialism }
				multiply_variable = { socialt2 = 0.01 }
				multiply_variable = { socialt2 = -0.2 }
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_politics_sore_oldl_fire_flame_tips
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { sore_oldl_war_engine_wood > 0 } }
					activate_mission = FRA_politics_sore_oldl_fire_flame
				}
				else = {
					clr_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_fire
					clr_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_opened
					set_country_flag = sore_oldl_war_engine_fade
					set_variable = { soncc = -3 }
					set_variable = { somcc = -3 }
					set_variable = { soicc = -3 }
					set_variable = { soscc = -3 }
					set_variable = { sowecc = -5 }
					set_variable = { sowewcc = -1 }
					activate_mission = FRA_politics_sore_oldl_fire_flame
				}
			}	
		}	
	}

			FRA_sore_oldl_goals_change = yes

	FRA_politics_sore_yout_plan_ing = {
		icon = generic_research
		allowed = {
			always = no
			tag = FRA
		}
		available = { NOT = { has_country_flag = youth_has_choosen_plan } }
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 14
		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_politics_sore_yout_plan_ing_tips
			set_temp_variable = { sypc = sore_yout_progress_change }
			add_to_temp_variable = { sypc = focus_sypcc }
			set_temp_variable = { sydc = sore_yout_danger_change }
			add_to_temp_variable = { sydc = focus_sydcc }
			set_temp_variable = { syqc = sore_yout_quality_change }
			add_to_temp_variable = { syqc = focus_syqcc }
			set_temp_variable = { syac = sore_yout_accept_change }
			add_to_temp_variable = { syac = focus_syacc }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { youth_futurism_scores > youth_mysticism_scores }
					check_variable = { youth_futurism_scores > youth_surrealism_scores }
					check_variable = { youth_futurism_scores > youth_ultramaterialism_scores }
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { syqc = 0.2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { youth_mysticism_scores > youth_futurism_scores }
					check_variable = { youth_mysticism_scores > youth_surrealism_scores }
					check_variable = { youth_mysticism_scores > youth_ultramaterialism_scores }
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { sydc = -0.2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { youth_surrealism_scores > youth_futurism_scores }
					check_variable = { youth_surrealism_scores > youth_mysticism_scores }
					check_variable = { youth_surrealism_scores > youth_ultramaterialism_scores }
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { syac = 0.2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { youth_ultramaterialism_scores > youth_futurism_scores }
					check_variable = { youth_ultramaterialism_scores > youth_mysticism_scores }
					check_variable = { youth_ultramaterialism_scores > youth_surrealism_scores }
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { sypc = 0.2 }
			}
			FRA_sore_yout_goals_change = yes
			hidden_effect = { activate_mission = FRA_politics_sore_yout_plan_ing }
		}
	}

		icon = SOV_place_hq
		allowed = {
			always = no
			tag = FRA
		}
		available = { always = no }
		is_good = yes
		fixed_random_seed = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = {
			FRA_govern_change = yes

			subtract_from_temp_variable = { pp = 50 }
			add_political_power = pp

			set_temp_variable = { FRA_politics_points_change = govern_central_control }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { FRA_politics_points_change = 50 }
			divide_temp_variable = { FRA_politics_points_change = 5 }
			FRA_politics_points_change = yes

			set_temp_variable = { ac = govern_central_control }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ac = 50 }
			divide_temp_variable = { ac = 40 }
			set_temp_variable = { wc = ac }
			set_temp_variable = { pc = ac }
			set_temp_variable = { mc = ac }
			set_temp_variable = { sc = ac }
			set_temp_variable = { fc = ac }
			FRA_social_politic_situation_change = yes

			hidden_effect = { activate_mission = FRA_govern_buff_change }		
		}	
	}

EUP_decisions_category = {
	EUP_union_time_change = {
		icon = SWI_no_elected_president
		activation = { always = no }
		allowed = { tag = FRA }
		available = { always = no }
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { eup_unionc = -1 }
			set_temp_variable = { eup_eco_receivec = -1 }
			set_temp_variable = { eup_tech_receivec = -1 }
			set_temp_variable = { eup_mili_receivec = -1 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { EUP_discuss_agree < EUP_discuss_disagree } }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = EUP_focus_union }
					add_to_temp_variable = { eup_unionc = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = EUP_focus_econ }
					add_to_temp_variable = { eup_eco_receivec = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = EUP_focus_tech }
					add_to_temp_variable = { eup_tech_receivec = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = EUP_focus_mili }
					add_to_temp_variable = { eup_mili_receivec = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = EUP_focus_union }
					add_to_temp_variable = { eup_unionc = 4 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = EUP_focus_econ }
					add_to_temp_variable = { eup_eco_receivec = 4 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = EUP_focus_tech }
					add_to_temp_variable = { eup_tech_receivec = 4 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = EUP_focus_mili }
					add_to_temp_variable = { eup_mili_receivec = 4 }
				}
			}
			EUP_variable_change = yes
			activate_mission = EUP_union_time_change
		}
	}

	EUP_change_focuses = {
		icon = generic_operation
		visible = { 
			has_completed_focus = FRA_independent_states
		}
		cost = 5
		days_re_enable = 0
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = eupun.1
		}
	}
}
